2. Apply UMAP embedding

https://www.rdocumentation.org/packages/uwot/versions/0.1.11/topics/umap


library(umap)
# install.packages('Rcpp')
any(is.na(df_strain))

set.seed(1)
umap_strain <- umap(df_strain)

umap_coordinate <- umap_strain$layout
colnames(umap_coordinate) <- c("UMAP1", "UMAP2")
class(umap_coordinate)
umap_coordinate <- as.data.frame(umap_coordinate)

ggplot(umap_coordinate, aes(x = UMAP1, y = UMAP2)) +
    xlab("\n umap1") + ylab("umap2 \n") +
    geom_point(shape = 16, size = 3, alpha = 0.9,

plot_UMAP <- function(strain_set) {
    umap_subset <- umap_coordinate[strain_set,
        ]
    ggplot(umap_subset, aes(x = UMAP1, y = UMAP2)) +
        xlab("\n umap1") + ylab("umap2 \n") +
        geom_point(shape = 16, size = 3,
            alpha = 0.9, color = "royalblue") +
        # scale_fill_manual(values =
        # my_color_collection)+
    ggtitle(paste0("UMAP coordination", " \n")) +
        scale_x_continuous(limits = c(-7,
            10)) + scale_y_continuous(limits = c(-11,
        10)) + theme(legend.text = element_text(size = 13)) +
        # theme(legend.position='top')
        # +
        # theme(legend.title=element_blank())
        # +
    mytheme_2d
}

plot_UMAP_all <- function(strain_set, i) {
    umap_color <- umap_coordinate
    umap_color$Color = ifelse(rownames(umap_color) %in%
        strain_set, "Selected", "Other strains")
    umap_color <- as.data.frame(umap_color)

    ggplot(umap_color, aes(x = UMAP1, y = UMAP2)) +
        xlab("umap1") + ylab("umap2") + geom_point(shape = 16,
        alpha = 0.9, aes(color = Color, size = Color)) +
        # scale_size(range = c(2, 5)) +
    scale_color_manual(values = c("blue",
        "red")) + ggtitle(paste0("mix", i)) +
        scale_x_continuous(limits = c(-7,
            10)) + scale_y_continuous(limits = c(-11,
        10)) + theme(legend.text = element_text(size = 13)) +
        # theme(legend.position='top')
        # +
        # theme(legend.title=element_blank())
        # +
    mytheme_2d
}

umap_coordinate
dim(umap_coordinate)
rownames(umap_coordinate)

vec_pool_strains <- rownames(umap_coordinate)  # 84 strains

# sample from 84 strains execute
# function
sampling_func_pool <- function(umap_coordinate,
    rand_num, vec_pool_strains, n, lower_percentile) {
    # empty list
    sampling20_list <- list()

    # do sampling for rand_num of times
    for (rand in 1:rand_num) {
        # print(rand) random sampling
        strain20_rand <- sample(vec_pool_strains,
            n)
        strain20_coor <- umap_coordinate[strain20_rand,
            ]
        strain20_dist <- rdist(strain20_coor)
        dim(strain20_dist)
        strain20_dist <- as.data.frame(strain20_dist)
        rownames(strain20_dist) <- rownames(strain20_coor)
        colnames(strain20_dist) <- rownames(strain20_coor)
        head(strain20_dist)

        # get minimum distance (minimum
        # positive)
        nearest_dist_vec <- apply(strain20_dist,
            1, FUN = function(x) {
                min(x[x > 0])
            })
        nearest_dist_vec <- nearest_dist_vec[order(nearest_dist_vec)]  # order from lowest to highest

        # nearest distance for lower
        # percentile
        nearest_dist_vec[1:round(n * lower_percentile)]
        # get mean of nearest UMAP
        # distance
        mean1 = mean(nearest_dist_vec[1:round(n *
            lower_percentile)])

        # save in list
        sampling20_list[[rand]] <- list(mean_nearest_distance = mean1,
            distance_mat = strain20_dist)
    }
    return(sampling20_list)
}

# combinations function (slight
# modification of sampling function)
mix_selection_pool <- function(umap_coordinate,
    rand_num, vec_pool_strains, n, lower_percentile) {
    # Sampling
    strain20_per <- sampling_func_pool(umap_coordinate,
        rand_num, vec_pool_strains, n, lower_percentile)
    # Distance
    mean_nearest_dist_vec <- c()
    for (i in 1:rand_num) {
        mean_nearest_dist_vec[i] <- strain20_per[[i]]$mean_nearest_distance
    }

    max_set <- strain20_per[[which.max(mean_nearest_dist_vec)]]$distance_mat  # matrices
    max_30strain_list <- rownames(max_set)  # strain_id
    max_dist <- strain20_per[[which.max(mean_nearest_dist_vec)]]$mean_nearest_distance  # nearest distance

    # plot strain20_30per <-
    # phylo_Biobank %>% filter(phy_id
    # %in% max_30strain_list)
    # plot_UMAP(strain66 %>%
    # filter(phy_id %in%
    # max_30strain_list))

    # return list
    l_set <- list(n = n, mix = max_30strain_list,
        dist = max_dist)
    return(l_set)
}

# testing if it works
sampling_func_pool(umap_coordinate, rand_num = 100,
    vec_pool_strains, n = 4, lower_percentile = 0.3)
mix_selection_pool(umap_coordinate, rand_num = 100,
    vec_pool_strains, n = 2, lower_percentile = 0.3)

    lower_percentile = 0.3)
